Grammar:

Rule 0     S' -> prog
Rule 1     prog -> decl_list
Rule 2     decl_list -> empty
Rule 3     decl_list -> decl decl_list

Rule 35    for_stmt_closed -> for_header closed_stmt
Rule 36    while_cond -> WHILE ( opt_expr )
